	function show_carregando(){	
		document.getElementById("aviso_na_tela").style.display='block';
		document.getElementById("aviso_na_tela").style.height= document.getElementById("container").clientHeight + 'px';
		document.getElementById("loading").style.display='block';

	function hidde_carregando(){	
		document.getElementById("aviso_na_tela").style.display='none';
		document.getElementById("loading").style.display='none';
	
	}

	function show_carregando(){	
		document.getElementById("aviso_na_tela").style.display='block';
		document.getElementById("aviso_na_tela").style.height= document.getElementById("container").clientHeight + 'px';
		document.getElementById("loading").style.display='block';
	
	}
	
	
	function hidde_carregando(){	
		document.getElementById("aviso_na_tela").style.display='none';
		document.getElementById("loading").style.display='none';
	
	}
